\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Key, typename Mapped, typename Cmp\+\_\+\+Fn, typename Node\+\_\+\+And\+\_\+\+It\+\_\+\+Traits, typename \+\_\+\+Alloc$>$\newline
class \+\_\+\+\_\+gnu\+\_\+pbds\+::detail\+::\+PB\+\_\+\+DS\+\_\+\+RB\+\_\+\+TREE\+\_\+\+NAME$<$ Key, Mapped, Cmp\+\_\+\+Fn, Node\+\_\+\+And\+\_\+\+It\+\_\+\+Traits, \+\_\+\+Alloc $>$}
Red-\/\+Black tree. 

This implementation uses an idea from the SGI STL (using a {\itshape header} node which is needed for efficient iteration).
